# Scan Report: CMS.gov Scan —

- Issue: https://github.com/mgifford/open-scans/issues/165
- Submitted by: mgifford
- Scanned at: 2026-04-05T01:33:29.101Z
- Engines used: All engines (AXE, ALFA, Equal Access, AccessLint, QualWeb)
- Scan duration: 31.7 minutes
- Total URLs submitted: 100
- Accepted public URLs: 100
- Rejected URLs: 0
- 🎨 **Accessibility personalization (CSS media queries):**
  - 🌙 Dark mode: None of the scanned URLs support `prefers-color-scheme: dark`
  - ⚡ **Reduced motion:** 69 of 100 URLs (69%) support `prefers-reduced-motion: reduce`
  - 🔍 High contrast: None of the scanned URLs support `prefers-contrast: more`
  - 🖥️ **Forced colors:** 69 of 100 URLs (69%) support `forced-colors: active`
  - 🪟 Reduced transparency: None of the scanned URLs support `prefers-reduced-transparency: reduce`
- ALFA outcomes: 345629 passed, 4164 failed, 9108 cantTell, 5612 inapplicable
- axe outcomes: 73977 passed, 9 failed, 512 cantTell, 2944 inapplicable
- Equal Access outcomes: 141826 passed, 1633 failed (1136 unique, 497 duplicate), 1356 cantTell, 0 inapplicable
- AccessLint outcomes: 6069 passed, 279 failed (278 unique, 1 duplicate), 0 cantTell, 0 inapplicable
- QualWeb outcomes: 67118 passed, 219 failed, 5054 cantTell, 69 inapplicable
- Duplicate findings caught by later scanners: 4013

## 🔧 Most Common Issues (ALFA)

These ALFA accessibility issues appear most frequently across your pages:

| Rule | Pages Affected | Documentation |
|---|---:|---|
| [SIA-R111](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r111): Interactive elements have a sufficient target size | **69** of 100 | [View Rule](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r111) |
| [SIA-R61](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r61): Documents start with a level 1 heading | **69** of 100 | [View Rule](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r61) |
| [SIA-R73](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r73): Text spacing can be adjusted without loss of content | **69** of 100 | [View Rule](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r73) |
| [SIA-R1](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r1): id attributes are unique within the document | **27** of 100 | [View Rule](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r1) |
| [SIA-R4](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r4): Page has a descriptive title | **27** of 100 | [View Rule](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r4) |
| [SIA-R59](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r59): Document has at least one heading to identify its main content | **27** of 100 | [View Rule](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r59) |
| [SIA-R87](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r87): First focusable element is a skip link | **27** of 100 | [View Rule](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r87) |
| [SIA-R53](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r53): Headings follow a logical hierarchy | **4** of 100 | [View Rule](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r53) |
| [SIA-R78](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r78): Headings of same level have text content between them | **2** of 100 | [View Rule](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r78) |
| [SIA-R42](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r42): Elements with an explicit ARIA role have the required parent element | **1** of 100 | [View Rule](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r42) |

## 🔍 Cross-Page Patterns: Common HTML Issues

These HTML patterns cause the same accessibility errors across multiple pages. **Fix the pattern once in your codebase to fix it everywhere!**

### 🎯 Top Patterns to Fix (Highest Impact)

#### Pattern 1: Affects 69 page(s) - 69 occurrence(s)

**Scanner**: ALFA
**Rule**: [SIA-R111: Interactive elements have a sufficient target size](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r111)
**Issue**: Target has insufficient size

**HTML Pattern**:
```html
<a href="/about-cms" class="menu-item-link" data-drupal-link-system-path="node/132926" data-once="navigationLinkMatch">About CMS</a>
```

**XPath** (use in browser DevTools):
```
/a[@class="menu-item-link"]
```

**How to Replicate**:
1. Open any affected page in your browser
2. Press F12 to open DevTools
3. Go to Console tab
4. Run: `$x('/a[@class="menu-item-link"]')`
5. The element will be highlighted

**Affected Pages**:
- https://cms.gov/digital-service/findsupportgov
- https://cms.gov/
- https://cms.gov/digital-service/digital-accessibility
- https://cms.gov/data-research/monitoring-programs/improper-payment-measurement-programs/exchange-improper-payment-measurement-eipm/improper-payment-findings
- https://cms.gov/data-research/monitoring-programs/improper-payment-measurement-programs/medicare-part-c-ipm/error-rate-findings-results
- *...and 64 more page(s)*

## Detailed Failure Information (ALFA)

### https://cms.gov/digital-service/findsupportgov

#### Rule: [SIA-R111: Interactive elements have a sufficient target size](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r111)
**WCAG**: [SC 2.5.8](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/target-size-minimum) (Level AA)

**Failure 1:**
- First identified: 2026-04-05
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a href="/about-cms" class="menu-item-link" data-drupal-link-system-path="node/132926" data-once="navigationLinkMatch">About CMS</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="menu-item-link"]`

**Failure 2:**
- First identified: 2026-04-05
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a href="/digital-service" class="linked-breadcrumb" data-once="navigationLinkMatch">Digital Service at CMS</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="linked-breadcrumb"]`

**Failure 3:**
- First identified: 2026-04-05
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a href="/about-cms/web-policies-important-links/help" title="Help with File Formats and Plug-Ins" class="file-format-help" data-once="linkMatch">Help with File Formats and Plug-Ins</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="file-format-help"]`

**Failure 4:**
- First identified: 2026-04-05
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a href="https://www.medicare.gov/" class="footer-menu-item-link" title="Medicare.gov" data-once="navigationLinkMatch">Medicare.gov</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="footer-menu-item-link"]`

**Failure 5:**
- First identified: 2026-04-05
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a class="list-item-link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/company/centers-for-medicare-&-medicaid-services/" data-once="linkMatch">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="list-item-link"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R61: Documents start with a level 1 heading](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r61)
**WCAG**: Best Practice

**Failure 1:**
- First identified: 2026-04-05
- Message: The document does not start with a level 1 heading

#### Rule: [SIA-R73: Text spacing can be adjusted without loss of content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r73)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.4.12](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/text-spacing) (Level AA)

**Failure 1:**
- First identified: 2026-04-05
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is `normal` which will result in a line height of less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p class="ds-c-usa-banner__header-text">An official website of the United States governmen...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="ds-c-usa-banner__header-text"]`

**Failure 2:**
- First identified: 2026-04-05
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is `normal` which will result in a line height of less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p class="ds-c-usa-banner__action ds-u-align-items--center ds-u-md-display--none ds-u-display--flex">...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="ds-c-usa-banner__action ds-u-align-items--center ds-u-md-display--none ds-u-display--flex"]`

**Failure 3:**
- First identified: 2026-04-05
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is `normal` which will result in a line height of less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p>...</p>`
- XPath: `/p`

#### Rule: [SIA-R42: Elements with an explicit ARIA role have the required parent element](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r42)

### https://cms.gov/data-research/monitoring-programs/improper-payment-measurement-programs/exchange-improper-payment-measurement-eipm/improper-payment-findings

#### Rule: [valid-lang](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/valid-lang?application=playwright)
**Impact**: serious
**WCAG**: [SC 3.1.2](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/language-of-parts) (Level AA)

**Failure 1:**
- First identified: 2026-04-05
- Message: lang attribute must have a valid value
- HTML: `<span lang="X-NONE">[1]</span>`
- XPath: `a[href$="#_ftnref1"] > span[lang="X-NONE"]`
